    SELECT [s2].[Id], [s2].[ContentPageId], [s2].[ContentValue], [s2].[CreaDate], [s2].[CreaUser], [s2].[IsDeleted], [s2].[IsStatus], [s2].[LangId], [s2].[LoginCount], [s2].[ModDate], [s2].[ModUser], [s2].[OrderNo], [s2].[SpecId]
    FROM [SpecContentValue] AS [s2]
    WHERE [s2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t1] ON [s].[Id] = [t1].[SpecId]
WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
ORDER BY [s].[Id], [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t1].[Id]"
